28/11/2021, 11:17 - +91 75638 00245: #include "bits/stdc++.h"
using namespace std;
/*
#include <ext/pb_ds/assoc_container.hpp>
using namespace __gnu_pbds;
using ordered_set = tree<int, null_type, less<int>, rb_tree_tag, tree_order_statistics_node_update>;
*/

#define all(x) begin(x), end(x)
#define rall(x) rbegin(x), rend(x)
#define sz(x) (int)(x).size()

using ll = long long;
const int mod = 1e9+7;

struct UFDS {
    vector<int> link, siz;
    int cc;
    UFDS(int n) {
        siz.resize(n, 1);
        link.resize(n);
        iota(all(link), 0);
        cc = n;
    }
    int find(int x) {
        if (x == link[x])
            return x;
        return link[x] = find(link[x]);
    }
    void unite(int a, int b) {
        a = find(a), b = find(b);
        if (a == b)
            return;
        if (siz[a] < siz[b])
            swap(a, b);
        siz[a] += siz[b];
        link[b] = a;
        --cc;
    }
};

void solve(int tc) {
    int n, m;
    cin >> n >> m;
    UFDS uf(n);
    for (int i = 0; i < m; ++i) {
        int u, v;
        cin >> u >> v;
        uf.unite(u-1, v-1);
    }
    cout << m-(n-1)+uf.cc-1 << '\n';
}

signed main() {
    cin.tie(0)->sync_with_stdio(0);
    int tc = 1;
    //cin >> tc;
    for (int i = 1; i <= tc; ++i) solve(i);
    return 0;
}

#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;


int Find(vector<int>& hashSet, int val)
{

	int parent = val;

	while (parent != hashSet[parent]) {
		parent = hashSet[parent];
	}

	return parent;
}

void Union(vector<int>& hashSet,
		int first, int second)
{

	int first_father = Find(hashSet, first);

	int second_father = Find(hashSet, second);

	if (first_father != second_father)
		hashSet[first_father] = second_father;
}

void change(vector<vector<char> >& matrix,
			int x, int y, int n, int m)
{

	if (x < 0 || y < 0 || x > m - 1
		|| y > n - 1 || matrix[x][y] == '#')
		return;

	matrix[x][y] = '#';

	change(matrix, x + 1, y, n, m);
	change(matrix, x, y + 1, n, m);
	change(matrix, x - 1, y, n, m);
	change(matrix, x, y - 1, n, m);
}

void changeCorner(vector<vector<char> >& matrix)
{
	int m = matrix.size();
	int n = matrix[0].size();

	for (int i = 0; i < m; i++) {
		for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {

			if (i * j == 0 || i == m - 1
				|| j == n - 1) {

				if (matrix[i][j] == '.') {
					change(matrix, i, j, n, m);
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

int numIslands(vector<vector<char> >& matrix)
{

	if (matrix.size() == 0)
		return 0;

	int m = matrix.size();
	int n = matrix[0].size();

	changeCorner(matrix);
	
	vector<pair<int, int> > edges;

	for (int i = 0; i < m; i++) {
		for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {
			if (matrix[i][j] == '.') {
				int id = i * n + j;
				if (j + 1 < n) {
					if (matrix[i][j + 1] == '.') {

						int right = i * n + j + 1;
						edges.push_back(make_pair(id, right));
					}
				}
				if (i + 1 < m) {
					if (matrix[i + 1][j] == '.') {
						int down = (i + 1) * n + j;

						edges.push_back(make_pair(id, down));
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	vector<int> hashSet(m * n, 0);
	for (int i = 0; i < m * n; i++) {
		hashSet[i] = i;
	}

	for (auto edge : edges) {
		Union(hashSet, edge.first, edge.second);
	}

	int numComponents = 0;

	
	for (int i = 0; i < m * n; i++) {
		if (matrix[i / n][i % n] == '.'
			&& hashSet[i] == i)
			numComponents++;
	}

	return numComponents;
}

// Driver Code
int main()
{
	ios::sync_with_stdio(false); cin.tie(nullptr); 
	int t;
	cin>>t;
	while(t--)
	{
	    int n,m;
		cin>>n>>m;
		vector<vector<char>>mat(n,vector<char>(m));
		for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
		{
			for(int j=0;j<m;j++)
				cin>>mat[i][j];
		}
	
	    cout << numIslands(mat)<<endl;
	}
	
	return 0;
}

#include <iostream>
using namespace std;
int main()
{
    int t,n,r,l;
    string s;
    cin >> t;
    while (t--)
    {
        cin >> n;
        cin >> s;
        r=0;
        l=0;
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
        {
            if (s[i] == '(')
            {
                r++;
            }
            else
            {
                l++;
            }
        }
        if (r>=l)
        {
            cout << 2*l << endl;
        }
        else
        {
            cout << 2*r << endl;
        }
    }
}

#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

int main()
{
    int t;
    cin >> t;
    while (t--)
    {
        long long int n;
        cin >> n;
        long long sumeven = 0;
        long long sumodd = 0;
        long long int arr[n];
        for (long long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
        {
            cin >> arr[i];
        }

        long long output = 0;

        for (long long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
        {

            if (i % 2 == 0)
            {
                sumeven += arr[i];
            }
            else
            {
                sumodd += arr[i];
            }
        }
        output = sumodd > sumeven ? sumodd : sumeven;

        cout << output << endl;
    }
    return 0;
}

string removeDuplicates(string S)
{
	string ans = "";

	
	for (auto it : S) {

		
		if (ans.empty() or ans.back() != it)
			ans.push_back(it);

		
		else if (ans.back() == it)
			ans.pop_back();
	}


	return ans;
}


int main()
{
	int t;
	cin>>t;
	while(t--)
	{
	    string s;
	    cin>>s;
	    string res=removeDuplicates(s);
	    int len = res.length();
	    cout<<len<<endl;
	}
	return 0;
}

import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
static int count=0;
static boolean isPrime(int n)
{

if (n <= 1)
return false;

else if (n == 2)
return true;


else if (n % 2 == 0)
return false;

for (int i = 3; i <= Math.sqrt(n); i += 2)
{
if (n % i == 0)
return false;
}
return true;
}
private static void findsubsequences(String s,
String ans)
{
if (s.length() == 0) {
if(!ans.equals("")){
int n=Integer.parseInt(ans);
if(isPrime(n))
count++;
}
return;
}
findsubsequences(s.substring(1), ans + s.charAt(0));

findsubsequences(s.substring(1), ans);
}
public static boolean isNumeric(String str)
{
for (char c : str.toCharArray())
{
if (!Character.isDigit(c)) return false;
}
return true;
}
public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
{
Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in
);

findsubsequences(str,"");
System.out.println(count);

}

}

        tmp[s[i]].push_back(i);
    }

    queue<int> q;//index
    q.push(0);
    dis[0] = 0;
    vis[0] = true;

    while (!q.empty()) {
        int cur = q.front();
        q.pop();

        int x = cur - 1, x2 = cur + 1;

        for (int i = 0; i < tmp[s[cur]].size(); ++i) {
            if (!vis[tmp[s[cur]][i]]) {
                vis[tmp[s[cur]][i]] = true;
                dis[tmp[s[cur]][i]] = dis[cur] + 1;
                q.push(tmp[s[cur]][i]);
            }
        }
        tmp[s[cur]].clear();

        if (x2 < n) {
            if (!vis[x2]) {
                vis[x2] = true;
                q.push(x2);
                dis[x2] = dis[cur] + 1;
            }
        }
        if (x >= 0) {
            if (!vis[x]) {
                vis[x] = true;
                q.push(x);
                dis[x] = dis[cur] + 1;
            }
        }

    }

    cout << dis[n - 1] << "\n";
    return 0;
}

vector <ll> par;
vector <ll> rnk;

void init(ll n)
{
    par.resize(n);
    rnk.resize(n);

    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
    {
        par[i] = i;
        rnk[i] = 0;
    }
}

ll find(ll a)
{
    if (par[a] == a)
        return a;

    par[a] = find(par[a]);
    return par[a];
}

void unio(ll a, ll b)
{
    ll para = find(a);
    ll parb = find(b);

    if (para == parb)
        return;

    if (rnk[para] < rnk[parb])
        par[para] = parb;
    else if (rnk[para] > rnk[parb])
        par[parb] = para;
    else
    {
        par[parb] = para;
        rnk[para] ++;
    }

}


void solve() {

    cin >> n >> m;

    init(n);

    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++)
    {
        ll a, b;

        a--;
        b--;

        unio(a, b);
    }

    vector <pair<ll, ll>> cost;

    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
    {
        ll a;
        cin >> a;

        if (a < 0)
            continue;

        cost.push_back({a, i});
    }

    sort(cost.begin(), cost.end());

    set <ll> st1, st2;

    ll sum = 0;

    debug(cost);

    ll first = 0;

    for (int i = 0; i < cost.size(); i++)
    {
        ll p = find(cost[i].second);

        if (i == 0)
            first = cost[i].first;

        debug(p);

        if (st1.find(p) == st1.end())
        {
            sum += cost[i].first;
            st1.insert(p);
        }

        debug(sum);
    }

    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
    {
        st2.insert(find(i));
    }

    if (cost.size() == 0 && st2.size() == 1)
    {
        cout << "0" << endl;
        return;
    }

    debug(st1);
    debug(st2);

    if (st2.size() == st1.size())
    {

        cout << sum - first + (st1.size() - 1) * first << endl;

        // if (st1.size() == 1 && *st1.begin() == *st2.begin())
        //     cout << "0" << endl;
        // else

        //     auto it1 = st1.begin();

        //     {
        //         it1 ++;

        //     if (it1 == st1.end())
        //         cout << sum << endl;
        //     else
        //         cout << "-1" << endl;
        // }
    }
    else
        cout << "-1" << endl;

    return;
}

void dijkstra(ll src,vector<vector<pii>> &g,vi &dist,ll n,vi &edgeChoosen)
{
    priority_queue<pii,vector<pii>,greater<pii>> pq;
    
    pq.push({0,0});
    dist[0]=0;
    edgeChoosen[0]=0;

    while(!pq.empty())
    {
        pii p=pq.top();
        pq.pop();

        ll u=p.second;
        ll wie=p.first;

        if(dist[u]<wie)
            continue;
        
        for(auto nbr:g[u])
        {
            ll v=nbr.first;
            ll w=nbr.second;

            if(dist[v]>dist[u]+w)
            {
                dist[v]=dist[u]+w;
                pq.push({dist[v],v});
                edgeChoosen[v]=w;
            }
            else if(dist[v]==dist[u]+w && w<edgeChoosen[v])
            {
                edgeChoosen[v]=w;
            }
        }
    }
}

ll getParent(ll node,vi &parent)
{
    if(parent[node]==-1)
        return node;
    
    return parent[node]=getParent(parent[node],parent);
}

bool mergeSet(ll node1,ll node2,vi &parent)
{
    ll par1=getParent(node1,parent);
    ll par2=getParent(node2,parent);
    
    if(par1==par2)
        return 0;
    
    parent[par1]=par2;
    return 1;
}

ll kruskals(ll n,ll m,vector<pair<ll,pii>> &edges)
{
    vi parent(n,-1);
    ll i;
    sort(all(edges));
    ll cost=0;
    fo(i,m)
    {
        ll u=edges[i].second.first;
        ll v=edges[i].second.second;
        ll w=edges[i].first;
        debug(mp(u,v));
        if(mergeSet(u,v,parent))
        {
            debug(w);
            cost+=w;
        }
    }  

    return cost;

}

void solve()
{
    ll n,m,i;
    cin>>n>>m;

    vector<vector<pii>> g(n);
    vector<pair<ll,pii>> edges(m);
    fo(i,m)
    {
        ll x,y,w;
        cin>>x>>y>>w;
        g[x].pb({y,w});
        g[y].pb({x,w});
        edges[i]={w,{x,y}};
    }

    vi dist(n,inf);
    vi edgeChoosen(n);
    dijkstra(0,g,dist,n,edgeChoosen);

    ll cost1=0;
    fo(i,n)
    {
        if(dist[i]==inf)
        {
            cout<<"NO"<<endl;
            return;
        }
        cost1+=edgeChoosen[i];
    }

    ll cost2=kruskals(n,m,edges);

    debug(cost1);
    debug(cost2);

    if(cost2==cost1)
        cout<<"YES";
    else    
        cout<<"NO";
    cout<<endl;
    

}

ll fxp(ll a,ll b,ll m) {
    if(b==0)
        return 1;
    if(b%2==0)
        return fxp((a*a)%m,b/2,m);
    return (fxp(a,b-1,m)*a)%m;
}
ll m_m(ll a,ll b,ll m) 
{
    ll res=0;
    a=a%m;
    while(b)
    {
        if(b&1)
        {
            res+=a; 
            res=res%m;
        }
        a=(a*2)%m;
        b=b/2;
    }
    return res;
}

    if(k == 0) return 1;

    else return ans;

const ll M = 1e5+100;
ll h[M],c[M],n,r;
vl gr[M];
vl dist(M);

void dijkstra(){
    set<pair<pll,ll> > s;
    fo(M) dist[i] = lmax;
    s.insert(mp(mp(0,1),0));
    vl down(n+1,1e18);
    vl up(n+1,1e18);
    down[1] = up[1] = 0;
    while(!s.empty()){
        auto cur = *s.begin();
        // cout<<cur.ff.sec<<"()"<<cur.ff.ff<<"()\n";
        s.erase(s.begin());
        ll node = cur.ff.sec;
        ll d = cur.ff.ff;
        for(auto x: gr[node]){
            if(h[x] >= h[node]){
                ll cst = 0;
                if(cur.sec != 1) cst = c[node];
                if(d + cst < up[x]){
                    auto it = s.find(mp(mp(up[x],x),1));
                    if(it != s.end()) s.erase(it);
                    up[x] = d+cst;
                    s.insert(mp(mp(up[x],x),1));
                }
            }
            if(h[x] <= h[node]){
                ll cst = 0;
                if(cur.sec != -1) cst = c[node];
                if(d + cst < down[x]){
                    auto it = s.find(mp(mp(down[x],x),-1));
                    if(it != s.end()) s.erase(it);
                    down[x] = d+cst;
                    s.insert(mp(mp(down[x],x),-1));
                }
            }
        }
    }
    ll ans = min(down[n],up[n]);
    if(ans == 1e18) ans = -1;
    pr(ans);
}

void solve(){
    re n; re r;
    fo(n) re h[i+1];
    fo(n) re c[i+1];
    fo(r){
        ll x,y; re x; re y;
        gr[x].pb(y);
        gr[y].pb(x);
    }
    dijkstra();
}

int32_t main(){
    KOBE;
    ll t;
    t = 1;
    // re t;
    while(t--) solve();
}

#define all(x) begin(x), end(x)
#define rall(x) rbegin(x), rend(x)
#define sz(x) (int)(x).size()

using ll = long long;
const int mod = 1e9+7;

struct UFDS {
    vector<int> link, siz;
    int cc;
    UFDS(int n) {
        siz.resize(n, 1);
        link.resize(n);
        iota(all(link), 0);
        cc = n;
    }
    int find(int x) {
        if (x == link[x])
            return x;
        return link[x] = find(link[x]);
    }
    void unite(int a, int b) {
        a = find(a), b = find(b);
        if (a == b)
            return;
        if (siz[a] < siz[b])
            swap(a, b);
        siz[a] += siz[b];
        link[b] = a;
        --cc;
    }
};

void solve(int tc) {
    int n, m;
    cin >> n >> m;
    UFDS uf(n);
    for (int i = 0; i < m; ++i) {
        int u, v;
        cin >> u >> v;
        uf.unite(u-1, v-1);
    }
    cout << m-(n-1)+uf.cc-1 << '\n';
}

signed main() {
    cin.tie(0)->sync_with_stdio(0);
    int tc = 1;
    //cin >> tc;
    for (int i = 1; i <= tc; ++i) solve(i);
    return 0;
}

#define pb                   push_back
#define F                    first
#define S                    second
#define all(v)               v.begin(),v.end()

template<class T> bool umin(T &a, T b) { return a > b ? (a = b, true) : false; }
template<class T> bool umax(T &a, T b) { return a < b ? (a = b, true) : false; }

void stugs(){
    ios_base::sync_with_stdio(0); cin.tie(0); cout.tie(0);
}

void solve(){
    int n,m,k;
    cin>>n>>m>>k;
    vector<int> graph[n+5];
    for(int i=0;i<m;i++){
        int u,v;
        cin>>u>>v;
        graph[u].pb(v);
        graph[v].pb(u);
    }
    vector<int> a(k);
    vector<int> dist(n+5,1e9);
    for(int i=0;i<k;i++){
        cin>>a[i];dist[a[i]]=0;
    }
    int tmp=1;
    queue<pair<int,int>> q;
    for(int i=0;i<k;i++){
        q.push({a[i],0});
    }
    while(q.size()){
        auto x=q.front();q.pop();
        for(auto y:graph[x.F]){
            if(dist[y]>x.S+1){
                dist[y]=x.S+1;
                q.push({y,x.S+1});
            }
        }
    }
    int Q;
    cin>>Q;
    while(Q--){
        int u;
        cin>>u;
        int x=dist[u];
        if(x==1e9){
            cout<<-1<<endl;
        }
        else{
            cout<<x<<endl;
        }
    }
}

int32_t main(){
    
    stugs();
    w(t)
    solve();
    return 0;
}

21/12/2021, 10:05 - PIYUSH: class Lamp {
  
  // stores the value for light
  // true if light is on
  // false if light is off
  boolean isOn;

  // method to turn on the light
  void turnOn() {
    isOn = true;
    System.out.println("Light on? " + isOn);

  }

  // method to turnoff the light
  void turnOff() {
    isOn = false;
    System.out.println("Light on? " + isOn);
  }
}

class Main {
  public static void main(String[] args) {

    // create objects led and halogen
    Lamp led = new Lamp();
    Lamp halogen = new Lamp();

    // turn on the light by
    // calling method turnOn()
    led.turnOn();

    // turn off the light by
    // calling method turnOff()
    halogen.turnOff();
  }
}

The Smallest Pair 

#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

int main() 
{
    long long h;
    cin>>h;
    while(h--)
    {
        long long p;
        cin>>p;
        vector<int>v(p);
        for(int a=0;a<p;a++)
        {
            cin>>v[a];
        }
        sort(v.begin(),v.end());
        cout<<v[0]+v[1]<<endl;
    }
	
	return 0;
}

int32_t main() {
    FAST

 int t=1;
   cin>>t;
   while(t--){
      map<int , int> mx;
      map<int , int> my;
      int n;
      cin>>n;
      int ref = 4*n - 1;
      while(ref--){
         int a,b;
         cin>>a>>b;
         mx[a]++;
         my[b]++;
      }
      for(auto pr : mx){

      }
      for(auto pr : my){
         if(pr.second%2 == 1){cout<<pr.first<<endl; break;}
      }
   }
   return 0;
}


Qualifying to Pre-Elimination

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
#define ll long long int 
#define vi vector<int>
#define vll vector<long long int>
using namespace std;

void solve()
{
    ll n,k;    cin>>n>>k;
    vll v(n);
    for(int  i=0;i<n;i++)
        cin>>v[i];
    sort(v.begin(),v.end(),greater<>());
    ll score = v[k-1],count=0;
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
    {
        if(v[i]>=score) count++;
        else    break;
    }
    cout<<count<<endl;
}

int main()
{
    int T;  
    cin>>T;
    for(int c=1;c<T+1; c++)
    {
        solve();
    }

    return 0;    
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;


#define fastio ios_base::sync_with_stdio(0); cin.tie(0); cout.tie(0);
#define endl "\n"

#define ll long long 
#define ld long double
#define vll vector<ll>
#define vv vector<vll>
#define pb push_back
#define lb lower_bound
#define ub upper_bound
#define pll pair<ll,ll>
#define vpll vector<pll>
#define ff first
#define ss second
#define tll tuple<ll,ll,ll>
#define vtll vector<tll> 
#define mt make_tuple
#define rep(i,a,b) for(ll i=a;i<b;i++)
#define rrep(i,a,b) for(ll i=a;i>=b;i--)
#define vect(a,n) vll a(n); rep(i,0,n) cin>>a[i];
#define all(a) a.begin(),a.end()
#define sortall(a) sort(a.begin(),a.end());


#define printv(a) rep(i,0,a.size()) cout<<a[i]<<" "; cout<<endl;
#define pairout(p) cout<<"("<<p.ff<<","<<p.ss<<")  "<<endl;
#define watch(x) cout<<(#x)<<"="<<x<<endl;

const ll INF = 1e18;
const ll MOD = 1e9 + 7;
const ll mod = 998244353;


void solve()
{ 
    ll n; cin>>n;
    map<string,ll> m;
    rep(i,0,3*n)
    {
        string s; cin>>s;
        ll x; cin>>x;
        m[s]+=x;
    }
    
    vll v;
    for(auto x:m) v.pb(x.ss);
    sortall(v);
    printv(v);
}

int main() 
{
    fastio;
    ll tc; cin>>tc; while(tc--)
    solve();
}


ChefWatson uses Social Network


#include <iostream>
#include <string>
#include <queue>
#include <vector>
#include <algorithm>
 
using namespace std;


/*bool cmp(pair<int,int> lhs,pair<int,int> rhs){
	return lhs.second < rhs.second;
}
*/
class cmp{
	public:
		bool operator()(const pair<int,int> & lhs, const pair<int,int>& rhs){
			return lhs.second < rhs.second;
		}
};
/*

struct cmpare{
    bool operator()(std::pair<int, int> lhs, std::pair<int, int> rhs) const{
        return lhs.second < rhs.second;
    }
} Compare;
 */
int main(){
 
	int noOffriends=0;
	int nposts=0;
	
	cin >> noOffriends;
	//cout << noOffriends;
	cin >> nposts;
	//cout << nposts;
	
	int friends[noOffriends];
	for(int i=0;i!=noOffriends;i++){
		cin >> friends[i];
		//cout << friends[i];
	}
	int posts[2][nposts];
	string str[nposts];
	int maxpop=0;
	for(int i=0;i!=nposts;i++){
		cin >> posts[0][i];
		cin >> posts[1][i];
		cin >> str[i];
		//cout << posts[0][i] << posts[1][i];
		//cout << str[i];
	}
	maxpop=100000;
	int kor[nposts];
	int order[nposts];
	for(int i=0;i!=nposts;i++){
		kor[i]=i;
		for(int j=0;j!=noOffriends;j++){
			if(posts[0][i]==friends[j]){
				order[i]=posts[1][i]+maxpop;
				break;
			}else{
				order[i]=posts[1][i];
			}
		}
	}
	
 	
	std::priority_queue<std::pair<int, int>, std::vector<std::pair<int, int> >, cmp> max_heap;
    
    for(int i=0;i!=nposts;i++){
    	max_heap.push(std::make_pair(kor[i],order[i]));
    }
    string stppr[nposts];
    for(int i=0;i!=nposts;i++){
    	stppr[i]=str[max_heap.top().first];
    	
    	max_heap.pop();
    }
 
 	for (int i = 0; i < nposts; ++i)
 	{
 		/* code */
 		cout << stppr[i] <<"\n";
 	}
 
	return 0;
}

Students and Fighting


#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

int main()
{
    int t;
    cin >> t;
    while (t--)
    {
        int n;
        cin >> n;
        int a[n];
        int count = 0;

        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
        {
            cin >> a[i];
        }
        sort(a, a + n);

        int ans = *max_element(a, a + n);

        if (a[n - 2] < ans)
        {
            cout << "peace:)" << endl;
        }
        else if (a[n - 2] == ans)
        {
            cout << "fight:(" << endl;
        }
    }

    return 0;
}

STACKS


#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

int main() {
	int t;
	cin>>t;
	while(t--){
	    long long int n, N=0;
	    cin>>n;
	    multiset<long long int> s1;
	    long long int arr[n];
	    
	    for(int i=0; i<n; i++){
	        long long int x, insert=0;
	        cin>>x;
	        arr[i] = x;

	    }
	    s1.insert(arr[0]);
	    for(int i=1; i<n; i++){
	        auto it = s1.lower_bound(arr[i]+1);
	        
	        if(it!=s1.end()){
	            
	            s1.erase(it);
	            s1.insert(arr[i]);
	            
	        } else{
	            s1.insert(arr[i]);
	        }
	    }
	    
	    cout<<s1.size()<<" ";
	    for(long long int ele: s1){
	        cout<<ele<<" ";
	    }
	   //cout<<*s1.lower_bound(5);
	    cout<<endl;

	}
	return 0;
}


ASHIGIFT

#include <iostream>
#include <map>
#include <vector>
#include <cassert>
#define ll long long
#define Map map<ll, A>
#define tr(c, i) for(typeof((c).begin()) i = (c).begin(); i != (c).end(); i++)

using namespace std;

typedef struct A {
    ll type;
    ll clan_req;
    ll clan_add;
    ll sub;
    public:
    A(ll t, ll a, ll b, ll c) : type(t), clan_req(a), clan_add(b), sub(c) { }
} A;

bool ispos(ll num, Map& M) {
    ll cnt = num;
    tr(M, it) {
	if ((*it).second.type == 0) {
	    if ((*it).second.sub < cnt) {
		cnt -= (*it).second.sub;
	    } else {
		return false;
	    }
	} else {
	    if ((*it).second.clan_req <= cnt) {
		cnt += (*it).second.clan_add;
	    }
	}
    }
    return true;
}

int main() {
    ll t, x, y, p, q, r, c, d;
    cin >> t;
    while (t--) {
	cin >> d;
	cin >> c;
	Map M;
	ll ma = 0;
	for (ll i = 0 ; i < c; ++i) {
	    cin >> x >> y;
	    M.insert(make_pair(x, A(0, 0, 0, y)));
	    ma += y;
	}
	cin >> c;
	for (ll i = 0; i < c; ++i) {
	    cin >> p >> q >> r;
	    M.insert(make_pair(p, A(1, q, r, 0)));
	}
	//binary seach
	ll lo = 0;
	ll hi = 2 * (ma + 1);
	ll mid, ans = (ma+1);
	while (lo <= hi) {
	    mid = lo + ((hi - lo)/(1LL * 2));
	    if (ispos(mid, M)) {
		if (mid < ans) ans = mid;
		hi = mid - 1;
	    } else {
		lo = mid + 1;
	    }
	}
	//assert(!flag);
	//assert(ans != 1e16);
	cout << ans << endl;
    }
    return 0;
}


 LOWSUM 

#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
#define REP(i,x,y) for(long long i=x;i<y;i++)
#define F first
#define S second
#define pb push_back
#define MOD 1000000007
typedef long long ll;

typedef vector<vi>  vvi;
typedef vector<ll>  vll;
typedef pair<int,int> pii;
typedef pair<ll,ll> pll;
typedef vector<pii> vpii;

int main() {
	// your code goes here
	ios_base::sync_with_stdio(false);
	cin.tie(NULL);cout.tie(NULL);
	int t;
	cin>>t;
	while(t--)
	{ 
	  ll k,q;
	  cin>>k>>q;
	 
	    vll ans;  
	    ll MAX=10001;
	      vll a(k);
	      REP(i,0,k)
	      cin>>a[i];
	      
	      vll b(k);
	      REP(i,0,k)
	      cin>>b[i];
	      sort(a.begin(),a.end());
	      sort(b.begin(),b.end());
	     
	     REP(i,0,min(k,MAX))
	     {
	         REP(j,0,min(k,MAX/(i+1)))
	         ans.emplace_back(a[i]+b[j]);
	     }
	     sort(ans.begin(),ans.end());
	     while(q--)
	     {
	      ll s;
	      cin>>s;
	     cout<<ans[s-1]<<"\n";
	     }
	}
	return 0;
}


SNAKEEAT

#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

typedef long long ll;
#define ff first
#define ss second
#define endl "\n"
const ll mod = 1000000007;
const ll N = 1e5 + 1;
const ll INF = 1e18;

int main()
{

    ll T, n, k, a, b;
    cin >> T;
    while (T--)
    {
        ll q;
        cin >> n >> q;
        vector<ll> v(n + 1);
        for (ll i = 1; i <= n; i++)
            cin >> v[i];
        sort(v.begin(), v.end());
        ll dp[n + 1] = {0};
        for (ll i = 1; i <= n; i++)
            dp[i] = dp[i - 1] + v[i];

        while (q--)
        {
            cin >> k;
            auto it = lower_bound(v.begin(), v.end(), k);
            if (it == v.begin())
                cout << n << endl;
            else
            {
                ll index = it - v.begin();
                index--;
                // cout<<index<<endl;
                ll ans = n - index;
                ll lo = 0, hi = index;
                ll e = 0;
                while (hi >= lo)
                {
                    ll mid = (hi + lo) / 2;
                    ll sum = (index - mid + 1) * k - (dp[index] - dp[mid - 1]);
                    // cout<<mid<<" "<<sum<<endl;
                    if (mid - 1 >= sum)
                    {
                        e = index - mid + 1;
                        hi = mid - 1;
                    }
                    else
                        lo = mid + 1;
                }
                // cout<<ans<<endl;
                cout << ans + e << endl;
            }
            // cout<<endl;
        }
    }
    return 0;
}

#include <bits/stdc++.h>
#define ll long long
#define db double
#define fi first
#define se second
#define pb push_back
#define ppb pop_back
#define mk make_pair
#define pii pair<int,int>
#define pll pair<ll,ll>
#define all(a) a.begin(),a.end()
#define tm template<class dt>
using namespace std;
using vi = vector<int>;
using vl = vector<ll>;
using vb = vector<bool>;
using ull = unsigned long long;
const int MOD = 1e9 + 7;
const db eps = 1e-9;
const db pi = acos(-1.0);
const int iinf = INT_MAX;
const ll inf = LONG_MAX;
const long double f_inf = FLT_MAX;
#define debug(x) cout << #x << " " << x << "\n";
#define tC(t) for(int ti=1;ti<=t;ti++)
tm dt max_t(const dt &a,const dt &b){return (a>b)?a:b;}
tm dt min_t(const dt &a,const dt &b){return (a>b)?b:a;}
tm void swapx(dt &a,dt &b){a ^= b;b ^= a;a ^= b;}
// tm void swap(dt &a,dt &b){dt t = a;a = b;b = t;}
ll mod_a(ll a,ll b){a %= MOD;b %= MOD;return (((a + b) % MOD) + MOD) % MOD;}
ll mod_m(ll a,ll b){a %= MOD;b %= MOD;return (((a * b) % MOD) + MOD) % MOD;}
ll mod_s(ll a,ll b){a %= MOD;b %= MOD;return (((a - b) % MOD) + MOD) % MOD;}
auto Case = [](int ti)->string{
	string r = "";
	while(ti){r = (char)((ti % 10) + 48) + r;ti /= 10;}
	return "Case #" + r + ": ";
};

long long f(long long n){return n * (n+1) / 2;}

void Solve(int ti){
	int N,K,q;
	cin >> N >> K >> q;
	string S;
	cin >> S;
	int pS[N][2];
	for(int i=0;i<N;i++){
		pS[i][0] = ((S[i]=='0') ? 1 : 0) + (i ? pS[i-1][0] : 0);
		pS[i][1] = ((S[i]=='1') ? 1 : 0) + (i ? pS[i-1][1] : 0);
	}
	vi Sub_ar(N,0);
	vl prefixSum(N,0);
	for(int i=0;i<N;i++){
		int l = i,r = N-1,idx = 0;
		pii L = {(i ? pS[i-1][0] : 0),(i ? pS[i-1][1] : 0)};
		while(l<=r){
			int m = l + (r-l)/2;
			if((pS[m][0] - L.fi)<= K && (pS[m][1] - L.se)<= K){
				idx = max_t<int>(idx,m);
				l = m + 1;
			}else r = m - 1;
		}
		Sub_ar[i] = idx - i + 1;
		prefixSum[i] = (long long)Sub_ar[i] + (i ? prefixSum[i-1] : 0);
	}
	int L,R;
	for(int i=0;i<q;i++){
		cin >> L >> R;
		L--; R--;
		int l = L,r = R,idx = R + 1;
		while(l<=r){
			int m = l + (r-l)/2;
			if((Sub_ar[m] + m - 1) > R){
				idx = min_t<int>(idx,m);
				r = m - 1;
			}else l = m + 1;
		}
		long long G_c = R - idx + 1,C = 0;
		if(idx)C = prefixSum[idx-1] - (L ? prefixSum[L-1] : 0);
		C += (G_c * R - (f(R) - f(idx-1)) + G_c);
		cout << C << '\n';
	}
}


int main(){
	cin.tie(0)->sync_with_stdio(0);
	#ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
	freopen("input.txt","r",stdin);
	freopen("output.txt","w",stdout);
	#endif
	cout.precision(30);
	cout.setf(ios::fixed);
	auto ti_start = std::chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();

	int t;
	cin >> t;
	tC(t){
		Solve(ti);
	}

	auto ti_end = std::chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();
	std::chrono::duration<float> duration = ti_end - ti_start;
	#ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
	printf("[%0.3fms]",duration.count() * 1000.0f);
	#endif
	return 0;
}

#else
#define deb(...){}
#endif
#define int                  long long
#define w(t)                 int t; cin>>t; while(t--)
#define mod                  1000000007
#define pb                   push_back
#define F                    first
#define S                    second
#define all(v)               v.begin(),v.end()

template<class T> bool umin(T &a, T b) { return a > b ? (a = b, true) : false; }
template<class T> bool umax(T &a, T b) { return a < b ? (a = b, true) : false; }

void stugs(){
    ios_base::sync_with_stdio(0); cin.tie(0); cout.tie(0);
}

void solve(){
    int n,m;
    cin>>n>>m;
    vector<pair<int,int>> a(n),b(m);
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
        cin>>a[i].F>>a[i].S;
    }
    for(int i=0;i<m;i++){
        cin>>b[i].F>>b[i].S;
    }
    sort(all(a));sort(all(b));
    int i=0,j=0,ans=0;
    while(i<n and j<m){
        int l=max(a[i].F,b[j].F);
        int r=min(a[i].S,b[j].S);
        if(l<=r){
            ans+=(r-l);
        }
        if(a[i].S<b[j].S){
            i++;
        }
        else j++;
    }
    cout<<ans<<endl;
}

int32_t main(){
    
    stugs();
    solve();
    return 0;
}


PSORT3

#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

#define ull unsigned long long int

bool conditionSort(const pair<ull, ull> &x, const pair<ull, ull> &y)
{
    if (x.second == y.second)
        return (x.first < y.first);
    else
        return (x.second > y.second);
}

int main()
{
    ull size, i, j;
    cin >> size;
    vector<pair<ull, ull>> vect;
    ull a[size], b[size];
    for (i = 0; i < size; i++)
    {
        cin >> a[i];
    }
    for (i = 0; i < size; i++)
    {
        cin >> b[i];
    }
    for (i = 0; i < size; i++)
    {
        vect.push_back(make_pair(a[i], b[i]));
    }
    sort(vect.begin(), vect.end(), conditionSort);
    for (i = 0; i < size; i++)
    {
        cout << vect[i].first << " " << vect[i].second << " ";
    }
}


SRT 

#include <iostream>
#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

int minSwaps(int arr[], int n)
{
    // Create an array of
    // pairs where first
    // element is array element
    // and second element
    // is position of first element
    pair<int, int> arrPos[n];
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
    {
        arrPos[i].first = arr[i];
        arrPos[i].second = i;
    }
 
    // Sort the array by array
    // element values to
    // get right position of
    // every element as second
    // element of pair.
    sort(arrPos, arrPos + n);
 
    // To keep track of visited elements.
    // Initialize
    // all elements as not visited or false.
    vector<bool> vis(n, false);
 
    // Initialize result
    int ans = 0;
 
    // Traverse array elements
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
    {
        // already swapped and corrected or
        // already present at correct pos
        if (vis[i] || arrPos[i].second == i)
            continue;
 
        // find out the number of  node in
        // this cycle and add in ans
        int cycle_size = 0;
        int j = i;
        while (!vis[j])
        {
            vis[j] = 1;
 
            // move to next node
            j = arrPos[j].second;
            cycle_size++;
        }
 
        // Update answer by adding current cycle.
        if (cycle_size > 0)
        {
            ans += (cycle_size - 1);
        }
    }
 
    // Return result
    return ans;
}

int main() {
	int t;
	cin>>t;
	while(t--)
	{
	    int n;
	    cin>>n;
	    int a[n];
	    for(int i = 0;i<n;i++)
	    {
	        cin>>a[i];
	    }
	    cout<<minSwaps(a,n)<<endl;
	}
	return 0;
}
